 He said that working in a Bengali film is like returning home
 sushmita (38) ne ravivaar ko aabhushan ke ek showrooms ke launch ke avasar par kaha, 'chaar dinon baad main kolkata ja rahi hum apni pehali bangla film kii shooting karne lekar main behad utsahit hum
 It is like a homecoming for me, a return to my roots
 'tasveeron main dekhie sushmita sen kii bindaas lifeunhone bataaya ki pehle vah bangla filmon main kaam karne se ghabraati thim, lekin ab unhen koi dar nahin he
 He said, 'I can work in a Tamil film, i can work in a Telugu film, but i was afraid to work in a Bengali film
 ab aisa nahin he
 i am working with great actors and am very excited
 'dekhie, sushmita sen kii andekhi tasveerenfilm kaa nirdesan rashtriya puraskaar vijeta nirdeshak srijith mukherjee kar rahe hai

 is suchi main jeff bejos haalanki, is baar bhi pehle sthaan par kabiz rahe hai

 unke baad bill gates or warren baffate kaa sthaan he

 mukesh ambani (61 varsh) kii sampatti 2018 main 40
 1 billion dollars, which has increased to 50 billion dollars
 duniya ke amiron main pichley saal vah 19 wein sthaan par the or is saal vah chah sthaan upar chadhakar 13wein number par aa gayi hai

 wipro ke chairman azim premaji 22

 History of Bijnor Lok Sabha seat Bijnor Lok Sabha seat is one of the important seats of western Uttar Pradesh, that is why its history is also very interesting
 meerut, nagina, mujffarnagar jaise shaharon se judi is seat par shuruyaat main congress kaa dabadabaa rahaa tha
